def fused_linear_jsd_kernel(beta: float, ignore_index: int, temperature: float, student_logits: torch.Tensor, teacher_logits: torch.Tensor, *, _launcher=_default_pallas_launcher):
    """
    Compute JSD loss from pre-computed logits.

    This kernel is kept for unit testing the JSD computation in isolation.
    For memory-efficient fused linear + JSD, use fused_linear_jsd_fwd instead.
    """
    # src[fused_linear_jsd.py:123]: batch_size, _vocab_size = student_logits.size()
    batch_size, _vocab_size = student_logits.size()
    # src[fused_linear_jsd.py:110]: def fused_linear_jsd_kernel(
    # src[fused_linear_jsd.py:111]:     beta: float,
    # src[fused_linear_jsd.py:112]:     ignore_index: int,
    # src[fused_linear_jsd.py:110-150]: ...
    loss = getattr(_helion_fused_linear_jsd_kernel, '_helion_output_meta_cache_0', None)
    if loss is None:
        loss = _helion_fused_linear_jsd_kernel._helion_output_meta_cache_0 = student_logits.new_empty(batch_size, dtype=torch.float, device='meta')
    # src[fused_linear_jsd.py:126]: for tile in hl.tile(batch_size):
    _BLOCK_SIZE_0 = 128
    _RDIM_SIZE_1 = 256
    # src[fused_linear_jsd.py:126]: for tile in hl.tile(batch_size):
    # src[fused_linear_jsd.py:127]:     # Scale by temperature
    # src[fused_linear_jsd.py:128]:     student_scaled = student_logits[tile, :] / temperature
    # src[fused_linear_jsd.py:126-148]: ...
    loss = _launcher(_helion_fused_linear_jsd_kernel, ((64 + _BLOCK_SIZE_0 - 1) // _BLOCK_SIZE_0,), student_logits, teacher_logits, loss, torch.tensor([temperature], dtype=torch.float32 if isinstance(temperature, float) else torch.int32, device=student_logits.device), torch.tensor([beta], dtype=torch.float32 if isinstance(beta, float) else torch.int32, device=student_logits.device), _RDIM_SIZE_1, _output_indices=[2], _inplace_indices=[], _block_spec_info=[((128, None), (None, None)), ((128, None), (None, None)), ((128,), (None,)), None, None])
    # src[fused_linear_jsd.py:150]: return (loss / batch_size).sum()
    return (loss / batch_size).sum()

        # src[grpo_loss.py:216]: ref_logp_val = ref_logp[tile_b, tile_l]
        ref_logp_val = ref_logp[:, :]
        # src[grpo_loss.py:217]: kl = torch.exp(ref_logp_val - logp) - (ref_logp_val - logp) - 1
        v_23 = ref_logp_val - v_13_copy_0
        v_24 = jnp.exp(v_23)
        v_25 = ref_logp_val - v_13_copy_0
        v_26 = v_24 - v_25
        v_27 = jnp.array(1, dtype=jnp.float32)
        v_28 = v_26 - v_27
        # src[grpo_loss.py:219]: kl *= completion_mask[tile_b, tile_l]
        load_4 = completion_mask[:, :]
        v_29 = v_28 * load_4
        # src[grpo_loss.py:220]: per_token_loss += beta * kl
        v_30 = v_29 * beta
        v_22 = v_22_copy_0 + v_30
        # src[grpo_loss.py:221]: kl_loss[tile_b, tile_l] = kl
        kl_loss[:, :] = v_29[:4, :]
        # src[grpo_loss.py:215]: if beta != 0.0 and ref_logp is not None:
        # src[grpo_loss.py:216]:     ref_logp_val = ref_logp[tile_b, tile_l]
        # src[grpo_loss.py:217]:     kl = torch.exp(ref_logp_val - logp) - (ref_logp_val - logp) - 1
        # src[grpo_loss.py:215-221]: ...
        return v_22

    def _else_branch(v_13=v_13, v_22=v_22):
        return v_22
    v_22 = lax.cond(ne, _if_branch, _else_branch)
    # src[grpo_loss.py:223]: loss[tile_b, tile_l] = per_token_loss
    loss[:, :] = v_22[:4, :]
    # src[grpo_loss.py:224]: is_clipped[tile_b, tile_l] = (per_token_loss1 < per_token_loss2).float()
    v_32 = v_18 < v_19
    v_33 = lax.convert_element_type(v_32, jnp.float32)
    is_clipped[:, :] = v_33[:4, :]

def grpo_loss_forward(logits: torch.Tensor, selected_logits: torch.Tensor, old_logp: torch.Tensor | None, ref_logp: torch.Tensor | None, advantages: torch.Tensor, completion_mask: torch.Tensor | None, temperature: float, beta: float, eps_low: float, eps_high: float, *, _launcher=_default_pallas_pipeline_launcher):
    """
    Helion kernel for GRPO loss forward pass.

    Args:
        logits: Logits tensor of shape [B, L+1, V]
        selected_logits: Pre-computed selected logits of shape [B, L]
        old_logp: Old log probabilities of shape [B, L] or None
        ref_logp: Reference log probabilities of shape [B, L] or None
        advantages: Advantages of shape [B]
        completion_mask: Completion mask of shape [B, L] or None
        temperature: Temperature scaling factor
        beta: KL regularization weight
        eps_low: Lower clipping bound
        eps_high: Upper clipping bound

    Returns:
        Tuple of (loss, kl_loss, is_clipped, lse)
    """
    # src[grpo_loss.py:170]: B, L_ADD_1, V = logits.shape
    B, L_ADD_1, V = logits.shape
    # src[grpo_loss.py:171]: L = L_ADD_1 - 1
    L = L_ADD_1 - 1
    # src[grpo_loss.py:173]: logits = logits[:, :-1, :]  # [B, L, V]
    logits = logits[:, :-1, :]
    # src[grpo_loss.py:175]: loss = torch.zeros([B, L], dtype=torch.float32, device=logits.device)
    loss = torch.zeros([B, L], dtype=torch.float32, device=logits.device)
    # src[grpo_loss.py:176]: is_clipped = torch.zeros([B, L], dtype=torch.float32, device=logits.device)
    is_clipped = torch.zeros([B, L], dtype=torch.float32, device=logits.device)
    # src[grpo_loss.py:177]: kl_loss = torch.zeros([B, L], dtype=torch.float32, device=logits.device)
    kl_loss = torch.zeros([B, L], dtype=torch.float32, device=logits.device)
    # src[grpo_loss.py:178]: lse = torch.zeros([B, L], dtype=torch.float32, device=logits.device)
    lse = torch.zeros([B, L], dtype=torch.float32, device=logits.device)
    # src[grpo_loss.py:180]: for tile_b, tile_l in hl.tile([B, L]):
    _BLOCK_SIZE_0 = 128
    _BLOCK_SIZE_1 = 128
    # src[grpo_loss.py:180]: for tile_b, tile_l in hl.tile([B, L]):
    # src[grpo_loss.py:181]:     max_logits = hl.full([tile_b, tile_l], float("-inf"), dtype=torch.float32)
    # src[grpo_loss.py:182]:     sum_exp = hl.zeros([tile_b, tile_l], dtype=torch.float32)
    # src[grpo_loss.py:180-224]: ...
    _launcher(_helion_grpo_loss_forward, ((4 + _BLOCK_SIZE_0 - 1) // _BLOCK_SIZE_0, (512 + _BLOCK_SIZE_1 - 1) // _BLOCK_SIZE_1), logits, lse, selected_logits, old_logp, advantages, completion_mask, ref_logp, kl_loss, loss, is_clipped, torch.tensor([temperature], dtype=torch.float32 if isinstance(temperature, float) else torch.int32, device=logits.device), torch.tensor([eps_low], dtype=torch.float32 if isinstance(eps_low, float) else torch.int32, device=logits.device), torch.tensor([eps_high], dtype=torch.float32 if isinstance(eps_high, float) else torch.int32, device=logits.device), torch.tensor([beta], dtype=torch.float32 if isinstance(beta, float) else torch.int32, device=logits.device), _output_indices=[1, 7, 8, 9], _inplace_indices=[1, 7, 8, 9], _block_spec_info=[((128, 128, None), (None, 1, None)), ((128, 128), (None, 1)), ((128, 128), (None, 1)), ((128, 128), (None, 1)), ((128,), (None,)), ((128, 128), (None, 1)), ((128, 128), (None, 1)), ((128, 128), (None, 1)), ((128, 128), (None, 1)), ((128, 128), (None, 1)), None, None, None, None], _ds_pad_dims=[(0, 2, 128, 0)], _scratch_shapes=[((128, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((128, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem')], _pipeline_arg_indices=[0])
    # src[grpo_loss.py:226]: return loss, kl_loss, is_clipped, lse
    return (loss, kl_loss, is_clipped, lse)

def layer_norm_fwd(x: torch.Tensor, normalized_shape: list[int], weight: torch.Tensor, bias: torch.Tensor | None=None, eps: float=1e-05, *, _launcher=_default_pallas_launcher):
    """
    Performs 1D layer normalization on the input tensor using Helion.
    Args:
        x (torch.Tensor): Input tensor of shape [batch_size, dim], expected to be FP16.
        normalized_shape (list[int]): List containing the dimension to normalize over (should be length 1).
        weight (torch.Tensor): Learnable scale parameter of shape [dim].
        bias (torch.Tensor | None): Optional learnable bias parameter of shape [dim].
        eps (float, optional): Small value added to variance for numerical stability. Default is 1e-5.
    Returns:
        tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:
            - The layer-normalized output tensor of shape [batch_size, dim], in FP16.
            - Mean tensor of shape [batch_size], in FP32.
            - Reciprocal standard deviation tensor of shape [batch_size], in FP32.

def matmul_split_k(x: torch.Tensor, y: torch.Tensor, epilogue: Callable[[torch.Tensor, tuple[torch.Tensor, ...]], torch.Tensor]=lambda acc, tile: acc, *, _launcher=_default_pallas_fori_launcher):
    """
    Matrix multiplication kernel using split-K parallelism.
    This kernel splits the reduction (K) dimension into multiple fragments to improve
    parallelism and performance, especially for large K. The results from each split
    are accumulated atomically into the output tensor. An optional epilogue function
    can be applied to the accumulator, e.g., for adding bias.
    Args:
        x (torch.Tensor): Left input matrix of shape [m, k].
        y (torch.Tensor): Right input matrix of shape [k, n].
        epilogue (Callable, optional): Function applied to the accumulator and tile indices
            after the matmul. Defaults to identity (no change).
    Returns:
        torch.Tensor: Resulting matrix of shape [m, n].
    """
    # src[matmul_split_k.py:57]: m, k = x.size()
    m, k = x.size()
    # src[matmul_split_k.py:58]: k2, n = y.size()
    k2, n = y.size()
    # src[matmul_split_k.py:59]: assert k == k2, f"size mismatch {k} != {k2}"
    assert k == k2, f'size mismatch {k} != {k2}'
    # src[matmul_split_k.py:60]: out = torch.zeros(
    # src[matmul_split_k.py:61]:     [m, n], dtype=torch.promote_types(x.dtype, y.dtype), device=x.device
    # src[matmul_split_k.py:62]: )
    out = torch.zeros([m, n], dtype=torch.promote_types(x.dtype, y.dtype), device=x.device)
    # src[matmul_split_k.py:63]: split_k = hl.register_tunable("split_k", PowerOfTwoFragment(1, 256))
    split_k = 8
    # src[matmul_split_k.py:64]: k_block = helion.next_power_of_2(helion.cdiv(k, split_k))
    k_block = helion.next_power_of_2(helion.cdiv(k, split_k))
    # src[matmul_split_k.py:65]: for tile_m, tile_n, outer_k in hl.tile([m, n, k], block_size=[None, None, k_block]):
    _BLOCK_SIZE_0 = 16
    _BLOCK_SIZE_1 = 128
    _BLOCK_SIZE_2 = k_block
    # src[matmul_split_k.py:65]: for tile_m, tile_n, outer_k in hl.tile([m, n, k], block_size=[None, None, k_block]):
    # src[matmul_split_k.py:66]:     acc = hl.zeros([tile_m, tile_n], dtype=torch.float32)
    # src[matmul_split_k.py:67]:     for inner_k in hl.tile(outer_k.begin, outer_k.end):
    # src[matmul_split_k.py:65-72]: ...
    _launcher(_helion_matmul_split_k, ((64 + _BLOCK_SIZE_0 - 1) // _BLOCK_SIZE_0, (64 + _BLOCK_SIZE_1 - 1) // _BLOCK_SIZE_1, (1024 + _BLOCK_SIZE_2 - 1) // _BLOCK_SIZE_2), x, y, out, _BLOCK_SIZE_2, _output_indices=[2], _inplace_indices=[2], _block_spec_info=[((16, None), (0, None)), ((None, 128), (None, None)), ((16, 128), (0, None))], _ds_pad_dims=[(0, 1, 128, 127), (1, 0, 128, 127)], _scratch_shapes=[((16, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((16, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore'), ((128, 128), 'jnp.float32', 'vmem'), ((), None, 'dma_semaphore')], _pipeline_arg_indices=[0, 1])

def pallas_add_3d(x: torch.Tensor, y: torch.Tensor, *, _launcher=_default_pallas_fori_launcher):

def _helion_scalar_index_transpose(x, out):
    # src[test_pallas.py:2530]: out[tile_b.begin, tile_n, tile_m] = x[tile_b.begin, tile_m, tile_n].T
